rich-diff-level-one\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content='import { Environment, Lightformer } from \"@react-three/drei\";\n\nconst Lights = () =\u0026gt; {\n  return (\n    // group different lights and lightformers. We can use group to organize lights, cameras, meshes, and other objects in the scene.\n    \u0026lt;group name=\"lights\"\u0026gt;\n      {/**\n       * @description Environment is used to create a background environment for the scene\n       * https://github.com/pmndrs/drei?tab=readme-ov-file#environment\n       */}\n      \u0026lt;Environment resolution={256}\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;group\u0026gt;\n          {/**\n           * @description Lightformer used to create custom lights with various shapes and properties in a 3D scene.\n           * https://github.com/pmndrs/drei?tab=readme-ov-file#lightformer\n           */}\n          \u0026lt;Lightformer\n            form=\"rect\"\n            intensity={10}\n            position={[-1, 0, -10]}\n            scale={10}\n            color={\"#495057\"}\n          /\u0026gt;\n          \u0026lt;Lightformer\n            form=\"rect\"\n            intensity={10}\n            position={[-10, 2, 1]}\n            scale={10}\n            rotation-y={Math.PI / 2}\n          /\u0026gt;\n          \u0026lt;Lightformer\n            form=\"rect\"\n            intensity={10}\n            position={[10, 0, 1]}\n            scale={10}\n            rotation-y={Math.PI / 2}\n          /\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;/group\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;/Environment\u0026gt;\n\n      {/**\n       * @description spotLight is used to create a light source positioned at a specific point\n       * in the scene that emits light in a specific direction.\n       * https://threejs.org/docs/#api/en/lights/SpotLight\n       */}\n      \u0026lt;spotLight\n        position={[-2, 10, 5]}\n        angle={0.15}\n        penumbra={1} // the penumbra is the soft edge of a shadow cast by a point light\n        decay={0} // the amount the light dims as it moves away from the source\n        intensity={Math.PI * 0.2} // the light intensity\n        color={\"#f8f9fa\"}\n      /\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;spotLight\n        position={[0, -25, 10]}\n        angle={0.15}\n        penumbra={1}\n        decay={0}\n        intensity={Math.PI * 0.2}\n        color={\"#f8f9fa\"}\n      /\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;spotLight\n        position={[0, 15, 5]}\n        angle={0.15}\n        penumbra={1}\n        decay={0.1}\n        intensity={Math.PI * 3}\n class=\"rich-diff-level-one\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eVideoCarousel.jsx\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/summary\u003e \u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto rich-diff-level-one\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content='import gsap from \"gsap\";\nimport { useGSAP } from \"@gsap/react\";\nimport { ScrollTrigger } from \"gsap/all\";\ngsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);\nimport { useEffect, useRef, useState } from \"react\";\n\nimport { hightlightsSlides } from \"../constants\";\nimport { pauseImg, playImg, replayImg } from \"../utils\";\n\nconst VideoCarousel = () =\u0026gt; {\n  const videoRef = useRef([]);\n  const videoSpanRef = useRef([]);\n  const videoDivRef = useRef([]);\n\n  // video and indicator\n  const [video, setVideo] = useState({\n    isEnd: false,\n    startPlay: false,\n    videoId: 0,\n    isLastVideo: false,\n    isPlaying: false,\n  });\n\n  const [loadedData, setLoadedData] = useState([]);\n  const { isEnd, isLastVideo, startPlay, videoId, isPlaying } = video;\n\n  useGSAP(() =\u0026gt; {\n    // slider animation to move the video out of the screen and bring the next video in\n    gsap.to(\"#slider\", {\n      transform: `translateX(${-100 * videoId}%)`,\n      duration: 2,\n      ease: \"power2.inOut\", // show visualizer https://gsap.com/docs/v3/Eases\n    });\n\n    // video animation to play the video when it is in the view\n    gsap.to(\"#video\", {\n      scrollTrigger: {\n        trigger: \"#video\",\n        toggleActions: \"restart none none none\",\n      },\n      onComplete: () =\u0026gt; {\n        setVideo((pre) =\u0026gt; ({\n          ...pre,\n          startPlay: true,\n          isPlaying: true,\n        }));\n      },\n    });\n  }, [isEnd, videoId]);\n\n  useEffect(() =\u0026gt; {\n    let currentProgress = 0;\n    let span = videoSpanRef.current;\n\n    if (span[videoId]) {\n      // animation to move the indicator\n      let anim = gsap.to(span[videoId], {\n        onUpdate: () =\u0026gt; {\n          // get the progress of the video\n          const progress = Math.ceil(anim.progress() * 100);\n\n          if (progress != currentProgress) {\n            currentProgress = progress;\n\n            // set the width of the progress bar\n            gsap.to(videoDivRef.current[videoId], {\n              width:\n                window.innerWidth \u0026lt; 760\n                  ? \"10vw\" // mobile\n                  : window.innerWidth \u0026lt; 1200\n                  ? \"10vw\" // tablet\n                  : \"4vw\", // laptop\n            });\n\n            // set the background color of the progress bar\n            gsap.to(span[videoId], {\n              width: `${currentProgress}%`,\n              backgroundColor: \"white\",\n            });\n          }\n        },\n\n        // when the video is ended, replace the progress bar with the indicator and change the background color\n        onComplete: () =\u0026gt; {\n          if (isPlaying) {\n            gsap.to(videoDivRef.current[videoId], {\n              width: \"12px\",\n            });\n            gsap.to(span[videoId], {\n              backgroundColor: \"#afafaf\",\n            });\n          }\n        },\n      });\n\n      if (videoId == 0) {\n        anim.restart();\n      }\n\n      // update the progress bar\n      const animUpdate = () =\u0026gt; {\n        anim.progress(\n          videoRef.current[videoId].currentTime /\n            hightlightsSlides[videoId].videoDuration\n        );\n      };\n\n      if (isPlaying) {\n        // ticker to update the progress bar\n        gsap.ticker.add(animUpdate);\n      } else {\n        // remove the ticker when the video is paused (progress bar is stopped)\n        gsap.ticker.remove(animUpdate);\n      }\n    }\n  }, [videoId, startPlay]);\n\n  useEffect(() =\u0026gt; {\n    if (loadedData.length \u0026gt; 3) {\n      if (!isPlaying) {\n        videoRef.current[videoId].pause();\n      } else {\n        startPlay \u0026amp;\u0026amp; videoRef.current[videoId].play();\n      }\n    }\n  }, [startPlay, videoId, isPlaying, loadedData]);\n\n  // vd id is the id for every video until id becomes number 3\n  const handleProcess = (type, i) =\u0026gt; {\n    switch (type) {\n      case \"video-end\":\n        setVideo((pre) =\u0026gt; ({ ...pre, isEnd: true, videoId: i + 1 }));\n        break;\n\n      case \"video-last\":\n        setVideo((pre) =\u0026gt; ({ ...pre, isLastVideo: true }));\n        break;\n\n      case \"video-reset\":\n        setVideo((pre) =\u0026gt; ({ ...pre, videoId: 0, isLastVideo: false }));\n        break;\n\n      case \"pause\":\n        setVideo((pre) =\u0026gt; ({ ...pre, isPlaying: !pre.isPlaying }));\n        break;\n\n      case \"play\":\n        setVideo((pre) =\u0026gt; ({ ...pre, isPlaying: !pre.isPlaying }));\n        break;\n\n      default:\n        return video;\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleLoadedMetaData = (i, e) =\u0026gt; setLoadedData((pre) =\u0026gt; [...pre, e]);\n\n  return (\n    \u0026lt;\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;div className=\"flex items-center\"\u0026gt;\n        {hightlightsSlides.map((list, i) =\u0026gt; (\n          \u0026lt;div key={list.id} id=\"slider\" className=\"sm:pr-20 pr-10\"\u0026gt;\n            \u0026lt;div className=\"video-carousel_container\"\u0026gt;\n              \u0026lt;div className=\"w-full h-full flex-center rounded-3xl overflow-hidden bg-black\"\u0026gt;\n                \u0026lt;video\n                  id=\"video\"\n                  playsInline={true}\n                  className={`${\n                    list.id === 2 \u0026amp;\u0026amp; \"translate-x-44\"\n                  } pointer-events-none`}\n                  preload=\"auto\"\n                  muted\n                  ref={(el) =\u0026gt; (videoRef.current[i] = el)}\n                  onEnded={() =\u0026gt;\n                    i !== 3\n                      ? handleProcess(\"video-end\", i)\n                      : handleProcess(\"video-last\")\n                  }\n                  onPlay={() =\u0026gt;\n                    setVideo((pre) =\u0026gt; ({ ...pre, isPlaying: true }))\n                  }\n                  onLoadedMetadata={(e) =\u0026gt; handleLoadedMetaData(i, e)}\n                \u0026gt;\n                  \u0026lt;source src={list.video} type=\"video/mp4\" /\u0026gt;\n                \u0026lt;/video\u0026gt;\n              \u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\n\n              \u0026lt;div className=\"absolute top-12 left-[5%] z-10\"\u0026gt;\n                {list.textLists.map((text, i) =\u0026gt; (\n                  \u0026lt;p key={i} className=\"md:text-2xl text-xl font-medium\"\u0026gt;\n                    {text}\n                  \u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n                ))}\n              \u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\n            \u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\n          \u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\n        ))}\n      \u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\n\n      \u0026lt;div className=\"relative flex-center mt-10\"\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;div className=\"flex-center py-5 px-7 bg-gray-300 backdrop-blur rounded-full\"\u0026gt;\n          {videoRef.current.map((_, i) =\u0026gt; (\n            \u0026lt;span\n              key={i}\n              className=\"mx-2 w-3 h-3 bg-gray-200 rounded-full relative cursor-pointer\"\n              ref={(el) =\u0026gt; (videoDivRef.current[i] = el)}\n            \u0026gt;\n              \u0026lt;span\n                className=\"absolute h-full w-full rounded-full\"\n                ref={(el) =\u0026gt; (videoSpanRef.current[i] = el)}\n              /\u0026gt;\n            \u0026lt;/span\u0026gt;\n          ))}\n        \u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\n\n        \u0026lt;button className=\"control-btn\"\u0026gt;\n          \u0026lt;img\n            src={isLastVideo ? replayImg : !isPlaying ? playImg : pauseImg}\n            alt={isLastVideo ? \"replay\" : !isPlaying ? \"play\" : \"pause\"}\n            onClick={\n              isLastVideo\n                ? () =\u0026gt; handleProcess(\"video-reset\")\n                : !isPlaying\n                ? () =\u0026gt; handleProcess(\"play\")\n                : () =\u0026gt; handleProcess(\"pause\")\n            }\n          /\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;/button\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\n    \u0026lt;/\u0026gt;\n  );\n};\n\nexport default VideoCarousel;\n'\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003egsap\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efrom\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"gsap\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e;\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003euseGSAP\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efrom\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"@gsap/react\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e;\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan const Lights = () =&gt; {
  return (
    // group different lights and lightformers. We can use group to organize lights, cameras, meshes, and other objects in the scene.
    &lt;group name="lights"&gt;
      {/**
       * @description Environment is used to create a background environment for the scene
       * https://github.com/pmndrs/drei?tab=readme-ov-file#environment
       */}
      &lt;Environment resolution={256}&gt;
        &lt;group&gt;
          {/**
           * @description Lightformer used to create custom lights with various shapes and properties in a 3D scene.
           * https://github.com/pmndrs/drei?tab=readme-ov-file#lightformer
           */}
          &lt;Lightformer
            form="rect"
            intensity={10}
            position={[-1, 0, -10]}
            scale={10}
            color={"#495057"}
          /&gt;
          &lt;Lightformer
            form="rect"
            intensity={10}
            position={[-10, 2, 1]}
            scale={10}
            rotation-y={Math.PI / 2}
          /&gt;
          &lt;Lightformer
            form="rect"
            intensity={10}
            position={[10, 0, 1]}
            scale={10}
            rotation-y={Math.PI / 2}
          /&gt;
        &lt;/group&gt;
      &lt;/Environment&gt;

      {/**
       * @description spotLight is used to create a light source positioned at a specific point
       * in the scene that emits light in a specific direction.
       * https://threejs.org/docs/#api/en/lights/SpotLight
       */}
      &lt;spotLight
        position={[-2, 10, 5]}
        angle={0.15}
        penumbra={1} // the penumbra is the soft edge of a shadow cast by a point light
        decay={0} // the amount the light dims as it moves away from the source
        intensity={Math.PI * 0.2} // the light intensity
        color={"#f8f9fa"}
      /&gt;
      &lt;spotLight
        position={[0, -25, 10]}
        angle={0.15}
        penumbra={1}
        decay={0}
        intensity={Math.PI * 0.2}
        color={"#f8f9fa"}
      /&gt;
      &lt;spotLight
        position={[0, 15, 5]}
        angle={0.15}
        penumbra={1}
        decay={0.1}
        intensity={Math.PI * 3}
      /&gt;
    &lt;/group&gt;
  );
};

export default Lights;'><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">Environment</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-v">Lightformer</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@react-three/drei"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">Lights</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// group different lights and lightformers. We can use group to organize lights, cameras, meshes, and other objects in the scene.</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">group</span> <span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"lights"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c">       * <span class="pl-k">@description</span> Environment is used to create a background environment for the scene</span>
<span class="pl-c">       * https://github.com/pmndrs/drei?tab=readme-ov-file#environment</span>
<span class="pl-c">       */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-v">Environment</span> <span class="pl-c1">resolution</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">256</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">group</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c">           * <span class="pl-k">@description</span> Lightformer used to create custom lights with various shapes and properties in a 3D scene.</span>
<span class="pl-c">           * https://github.com/pmndrs/drei?tab=readme-ov-file#lightformer</span>
<span class="pl-c">           */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-v">Lightformer</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">form</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"rect"</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">intensity</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">position</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">scale</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">color</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">"#495057"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">/&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-v">Lightformer</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">form</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"rect"</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">intensity</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">position</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">scale</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">rotation-y</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">PI</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">/&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-v">Lightformer</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">form</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"rect"</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">intensity</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">position</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">scale</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">rotation-y</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">PI</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">/&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-s1">group</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-v">Environment</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

      <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/**</span>
<span class="pl-c">       * <span class="pl-k">@description</span> spotLight is used to create a light source positioned at a specific point</span>
<span class="pl-c">       * in the scene that emits light in a specific direction.</span>
<span class="pl-c">       * https://threejs.org/docs/#api/en/lights/SpotLight</span>
<span class="pl-c">       */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">spotLight</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">position</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">angle</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">0.15</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">penumbra</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c">// the penumbra is the soft edge of a shadow cast by a point light</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">decay</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c">// the amount the light dims as it moves away from the source</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">intensity</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">PI</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.2</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c">// the light intensity</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">color</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">"#f8f9fa"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">/&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">spotLight</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">position</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">25</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">angle</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">0.15</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">penumbra</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">decay</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">intensity</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">PI</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.2</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">color</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">"#f8f9fa"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">/&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">spotLight</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">position</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">15</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">angle</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">0.15</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">penumbra</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">decay</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">0.1</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">intensity</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">PI</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">/&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-s1">group</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-v">Lights</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div> </details></del><del><details class="rich-diff-level-zero"> <summary class="rich-diff-level-one"><code>materials</code></summary> <div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto rich-diff-level-one" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    useEffect(() =&gt; {
      Object.entries(materials).map((material) =&gt; {
        // these are the material names that can't be changed color
        if (
          material[0] !== &quot;zFdeDaGNRwzccye&quot; &amp;&amp;
          material[0] !== &quot;ujsvqBWRMnqdwPx&quot; &amp;&amp;
          material[0] !== &quot;hUlRcbieVuIiOXG&quot; &amp;&amp;
          material[0] !== &quot;jlzuBkUzuJqgiAK&quot; &amp;&amp;
          material[0] !== &quot;xNrofRCqOXXHVZt&quot;
        ) {
          material[1].color = new THREE.Color(props.item.color[0]);
        }
        material[1].needsUpdate = true;
      });
    }, [materials, props.item]);"><pre>    <span class="pl-en">useEffect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">entries</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">materials</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">material</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// these are the material names that can't be changed color</span>
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">material</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">!==</span> <span class="pl-s">"zFdeDaGNRwzccye"</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">material</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">!==</span> <span class="pl-s">"ujsvqBWRMnqdwPx"</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">material</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">!==</span> <span class="pl-s">"hUlRcbieVuIiOXG"</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">material</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">!==</span> <span class="pl-s">"jlzuBkUzuJqgiAK"</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">material</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">!==</span> <span class="pl-s">"xNrofRCqOXXHVZt"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">material</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">color</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">THREE</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">Color</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">props</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">color</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">material</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">needsUpdate</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">materials</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">props</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">item</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div> </details></del><del><details class="rich-diff-level-zero"> <summary class="rich-diff-level-one"><code>VideoCarousel.jsx</code></summary> <div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto rich-diff-level-one" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content='import gsap from "gsap";
import { useGSAP } from "@gsap/react";
import { ScrollTrigger } from "gsap/all";
gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);
import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";

import { hightlightsSlides } from "../constants";
import { pauseImg, playImg, replayImg } from "../utils";

const VideoCarousel = () =&gt; {
  const videoRef = useRef([]);
  const videoSpanRef = useRef([]);
  const videoDivRef = useRef([]);

  // video and indicator
  const [video, setVideo] = useState({
    isEnd: false,
    startPlay: false,
    videoId: 0,
    isLastVideo: false,
    isPlaying: false,
  });

  const [loadedData, setLoadedData] = useState([]);
  const { isEnd, isLastVideo, startPlay, videoId, isPlaying } = video;

  useGSAP(() =&gt; {
    // slider animation to move the video out of the screen and bring the next video in
    gsap.to("#slider", {
      transform: `translateX(${-100 * videoId}%)`,
      duration: 2,
      ease: "power2.inOut", // show visualizer https://gsap.com/docs/v3/Eases
    });

    // video animation to play the video when it is in the view
    gsap.to("#video", {
      scrollTrigger: {
        trigger: "#video",
        toggleActions: "restart none none none",
      },
      onComplete: () =&gt; {
        setVideo((pre) =&gt; ({
          ...pre,
          startPlay: true,
          isPlaying: true,
        }));
      },
    });
  }, [isEnd, videoId]);

  useEffect(() =&gt; {
    let currentProgress = 0;
    let span = videoSpanRef.current;

    if (span[videoId]) {
      // animation to move the indicator
      let anim = gsap.to(span[videoId], {
        onUpdate: () =&gt; {
          // get the progress of the video
          const progress = Math.ceil(anim.progress() * 100);

          if (progress != currentProgress) {
            currentProgress = progress;

            // set the width of the progress bar
            gsap.to(videoDivRef.current[videoId], {
              width:
                window.innerWidth &lt; 760
                  ? "10vw" // mobile
                  : window.innerWidth &lt; 1200
                  ? "10vw" // tablet
                  : "4vw", // laptop
            });

            // set the background color of the progress bar
            gsap.to(span[videoId], {
              width: `${currentProgress}%`,
              backgroundColor: "white",
            });
          }
        },

        // when the video is ended, replace the progress bar with the indicator and change the background color
        onComplete: () =&gt; {
          if (isPlaying) {
            gsap.to(videoDivRef.current[videoId], {
              width: "12px",
            });
            gsap.to(span[videoId], {
              backgroundColor: "#afafaf",
            });
          }
        },
      });

      if (videoId == 0) {
        anim.restart();
      }

      // update the progress bar
      const animUpdate = () =&gt; {
        anim.progress(
          videoRef.current[videoId].currentTime /
            hightlightsSlides[videoId].videoDuration
        );
      };

      if (isPlaying) {
        // ticker to update the progress bar
        gsap.ticker.add(animUpdate);
      } else {
        // remove the ticker when the video is paused (progress bar is stopped)
        gsap.ticker.remove(animUpdate);
      }
    }
  }, [videoId, startPlay]);

  useEffect(() =&gt; {
    if (loadedData.length &gt; 3) {
      if (!isPlaying) {
        videoRef.current[videoId].pause();
      } else {
        startPlay &amp;&amp; videoRef.current[videoId].play();
      }
    }
  }, [startPlay, videoId, isPlaying, loadedData]);

  // vd id is the id for every video until id becomes number 3
  const handleProcess = (type, i) =&gt; {
    switch (type) {
      case "video-end":
        setVideo((pre) =&gt; ({ ...pre, isEnd: true, videoId: i + 1 }));
        break;

      case "video-last":
        setVideo((pre) =&gt; ({ ...pre, isLastVideo: true }));
        break;

      case "video-reset":
        setVideo((pre) =&gt; ({ ...pre, videoId: 0, isLastVideo: false }));
        break;

      case "pause":
        setVideo((pre) =&gt; ({ ...pre, isPlaying: !pre.isPlaying }));
        break;

      case "play":
        setVideo((pre) =&gt; ({ ...pre, isPlaying: !pre.isPlaying }));
        break;

      default:
        return video;
    }
  };

  const handleLoadedMetaData = (i, e) =&gt; setLoadedData((pre) =&gt; [...pre, e]);

  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div className="flex items-center"&gt;
        {hightlightsSlides.map((list, i) =&gt; (
          &lt;div key={list.id} id="slider" className="sm:pr-20 pr-10"&gt;
            &lt;div className="video-carousel_container"&gt;
              &lt;div className="w-full h-full flex-center rounded-3xl overflow-hidden bg-black"&gt;
                &lt;video
                  id="video"
                  playsInline={true}
                  className={`${
                    list.id === 2 &amp;&amp; "translate-x-44"
                  } pointer-events-none`}
                  preload="auto"
                  muted
                  ref={(el) =&gt; (videoRef.current[i] = el)}
                  onEnded={() =&gt;
                    i !== 3
                      ? handleProcess("video-end", i)
                      : handleProcess("video-last")
                  }
                  onPlay={() =&gt;
                    setVideo((pre) =&gt; ({ ...pre, isPlaying: true }))
                  }
                  onLoadedMetadata={(e) =&gt; handleLoadedMetaData(i, e)}
                &gt;
                  &lt;source src={list.video} type="video/mp4" /&gt;
                &lt;/video&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;

              &lt;div className="absolute top-12 left-[5%] z-10"&gt;
                {list.textLists.map((text, i) =&gt; (
                  &lt;p key={i} className="md:text-2xl text-xl font-medium"&gt;
                    {text}
                  &lt;/p&gt;
                ))}
              &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;
        ))}
      &lt;/div&gt;

      &lt;div className="relative flex-center mt-10"&gt;
        &lt;div className="flex-center py-5 px-7 bg-gray-300 backdrop-blur rounded-full"&gt;
          {videoRef.current.map((_, i) =&gt; (
            &lt;span
              key={i}
              className="mx-2 w-3 h-3 bg-gray-200 rounded-full relative cursor-pointer"
              ref={(el) =&gt; (videoDivRef.current[i] = el)}
            &gt;
              &lt;span
                className="absolute h-full w-full rounded-full"
                ref={(el) =&gt; (videoSpanRef.current[i] = el)}
              /&gt;
            &lt;/span&gt;
          ))}
        &lt;/div&gt;

        &lt;button className="control-btn"&gt;
          &lt;img
            src={isLastVideo ? replayImg : !isPlaying ? playImg : pauseImg}
            alt={isLastVideo ? "replay" : !isPlaying ? "play" : "pause"}
            onClick={
              isLastVideo
                ? () =&gt; handleProcess("video-reset")
                : !isPlaying
                ? () =&gt; handleProcess("play")
                : () =&gt; handleProcess("pause")
            }
          /&gt;
        &lt;/button&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
};

export default VideoCarousel;
'><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"gsap"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">useGSAP</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"@gsap/react"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">ScrollTrigger</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"gsap/all"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">registerPlugin</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-v">ScrollTrigger</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">useEffect</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">useRef</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">useState</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">hightlightsSlides</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../constants"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">pauseImg</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">playImg</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">replayImg</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../utils"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-v">VideoCarousel</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">videoRef</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useRef</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">videoSpanRef</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useRef</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">videoDivRef</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useRef</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// video and indicator</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">video</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">setVideo</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useState</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">isEnd</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">startPlay</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">videoId</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">isLastVideo</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">isPlaying</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">loadedData</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">setLoadedData</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useState</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> isEnd<span class="pl-kos">,</span> isLastVideo<span class="pl-kos">,</span> startPlay<span class="pl-kos">,</span> videoId<span class="pl-kos">,</span> isPlaying <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">video</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-en">useGSAP</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c">// slider animation to move the video out of the screen and bring the next video in</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">to</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"#slider"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">transform</span>: <span class="pl-s">`translateX(<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>%)`</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">duration</span>: <span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">ease</span>: <span class="pl-s">"power2.inOut"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// show visualizer https://gsap.com/docs/v3/Eases</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

    <span class="pl-c">// video animation to play the video when it is in the view</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">to</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"#video"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">scrollTrigger</span>: <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">trigger</span>: <span class="pl-s">"#video"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">toggleActions</span>: <span class="pl-s">"restart none none none"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-en">onComplete</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">setVideo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          ...<span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">startPlay</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">isPlaying</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">isEnd</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-en">useEffect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">currentProgress</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">span</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">videoSpanRef</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">current</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">span</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c">// animation to move the indicator</span>
      <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">anim</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">to</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">span</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-en">onUpdate</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-c">// get the progress of the video</span>
          <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">progress</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">ceil</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">anim</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">progress</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">100</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

          <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">progress</span> <span class="pl-c1">!=</span> <span class="pl-s1">currentProgress</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">currentProgress</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">progress</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

            <span class="pl-c">// set the width of the progress bar</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">to</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">videoDivRef</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">current</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">width</span>:
                <span class="pl-smi">window</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">innerWidth</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">760</span>
                  ? <span class="pl-s">"10vw"</span> <span class="pl-c">// mobile</span>
                  : <span class="pl-smi">window</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">innerWidth</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">1200</span>
                  ? <span class="pl-s">"10vw"</span> <span class="pl-c">// tablet</span>
                  : <span class="pl-s">"4vw"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c">// laptop</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

            <span class="pl-c">// set the background color of the progress bar</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">to</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">span</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">width</span>: <span class="pl-s">`<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">currentProgress</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>%`</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">backgroundColor</span>: <span class="pl-s">"white"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

        <span class="pl-c">// when the video is ended, replace the progress bar with the indicator and change the background color</span>
        <span class="pl-en">onComplete</span>: <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">isPlaying</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">to</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">videoDivRef</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">current</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">width</span>: <span class="pl-s">"12px"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">to</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">span</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">backgroundColor</span>: <span class="pl-s">"#afafaf"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">anim</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">restart</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

      <span class="pl-c">// update the progress bar</span>
      <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">animUpdate</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">anim</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">progress</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">videoRef</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">current</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">currentTime</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">hightlightsSlides</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">videoDuration</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">isPlaying</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// ticker to update the progress bar</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">ticker</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">add</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-en">animUpdate</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c">// remove the ticker when the video is paused (progress bar is stopped)</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">gsap</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">ticker</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">remove</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-en">animUpdate</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">startPlay</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-en">useEffect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">loadedData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">isPlaying</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">videoRef</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">current</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">pause</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">startPlay</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-s1">videoRef</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">current</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">play</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">startPlay</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">videoId</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">isPlaying</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">loadedData</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// vd id is the id for every video until id becomes number 3</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-en">handleProcess</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">switch</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-s">"video-end"</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">setVideo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> ...<span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">isEnd</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">videoId</span>: <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-s">"video-last"</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">setVideo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> ...<span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">isLastVideo</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-s">"video-reset"</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">setVideo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> ...<span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">videoId</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">isLastVideo</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-s">"pause"</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">setVideo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> ...<span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">isPlaying</span>: <span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">isPlaying</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-s">"play"</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">setVideo</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> ...<span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">isPlaying</span>: <span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">pre</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">isPlaying</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
        <span class="pl-k">break</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

      <span class="pl-k">default</span>:
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">video</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
